\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00007}00007 \textcolor{comment}{provides an environment for the development of block }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00008}00008 \textcolor{comment}{preconditioners for the iterative solution of linear systems}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00009}00009 \textcolor{comment}{by Krylov subspace methods. The framework is based on the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00010}00010 \textcolor{comment}{classification of the problem's unknowns (degrees of freedom; here}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00011}00011 \textcolor{comment}{abbreviated as dofs)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00012}00012 \textcolor{comment}{into different "{}dof types"{} which, in a multi-\/physics context, }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00013}00013 \textcolor{comment}{typically represent different physical quantities. A key feature of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00014}00014 \textcolor{comment}{the framework is that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00015}00015 \textcolor{comment}{it allows existing block preconditioners (which were developed for a particular}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00016}00016 \textcolor{comment}{single-\/physics application, say) to be re-\/used, in a hierarchical }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00017}00017 \textcolor{comment}{fashion, in block preconditioners for related}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00018}00018 \textcolor{comment}{multi-\/physics problems. This means that existing Navier-\/Stokes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00019}00019 \textcolor{comment}{and solid mechanics preconditioners can be used to create}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00020}00020 \textcolor{comment}{preconditioners for fluid-\/structure interaction problems, say. }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00021}00021 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00022}00022 \textcolor{comment}{Following a brief overview of the underlying}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00153}00153 \textcolor{comment}{\(\backslash\)f]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00154}00154 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00155}00155 \textcolor{comment}{which requires the (exact or approximate) solution of the two }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00156}00156 \textcolor{comment}{smaller linear systems \(\backslash\)f\$ \{\(\backslash\)bf J\}\_\{xx\} \(\backslash\) \{\(\backslash\)bf z\_x\} = \{\(\backslash\)bf y\_x\}\(\backslash\)f\$}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00157}00157 \textcolor{comment}{and \(\backslash\)f\$ \{\(\backslash\)bf J\}\_\{yy\} \(\backslash\) \{\(\backslash\)bf z\_y\} = \{\(\backslash\)bf y\_y\}\(\backslash\)f\$.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00158}00158 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00159}00159 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00160}00160 \textcolor{comment}{\(\backslash\)section generic\_implementation Overview}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00161}00161 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00162}00162 \textcolor{comment}{The above example shows that the application of block preconditioners}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00163}00163 \textcolor{comment}{typically require several generic steps:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00164}00164 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00165}00165 \textcolor{comment}{-\/\# The classification of the dofs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00166}00166 \textcolor{comment}{-\/\# The application of subsidiary preconditioning operations such as }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00167}00167 \textcolor{comment}{   the solution of (smaller) linear systems or the evaluation of matrix-\/vector }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00168}00168 \textcolor{comment}{   products with some of the blocks that are extracted from the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00169}00169 \textcolor{comment}{   original linear system.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00170}00170 \textcolor{comment}{   }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00171}00171 \textcolor{comment}{The following subsections describe how these tasks are performed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00172}00172 \textcolor{comment}{within \(\backslash\)c oomph-\/lib's block preconditioning framework.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00173}00173 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00174}00174 \textcolor{comment}{\(\backslash\)subsection block\_preconditionable\_elements The classification of dof types via block preconditionable elements}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00175}00175 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00176}00176 \textcolor{comment}{The classification of dofs is specified by the elements since they are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00177}00177 \textcolor{comment}{the only objects within \(\backslash\)c oomph-\/lib's data structure }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00178}00178 \textcolor{comment}{that "{}know"{} what role a specific dof plays in "{}their"{} equations. }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00179}00179 \textcolor{comment}{During the setup phase, the block preconditioner loops over "{}all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00180}00180 \textcolor{comment}{elements"{} (specified via one or more \(\backslash\)c Meshes -\/-\/ here simply used as }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00181}00181 \textcolor{comment}{containers for elements; see below for further details) to establish the }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00182}00182 \textcolor{comment}{"{}dof type"{} for each global unknown.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00183}00183 \textcolor{comment}{ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00184}00184 \textcolor{comment}{To achieve this, the class \(\backslash\)c GeneralisedElement }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00185}00185 \textcolor{comment}{contains two broken virtual methods that must be re-\/implemented/overloaded to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00186}00186 \textcolor{comment}{label each of the element's dofs with its type. These methods are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00187}00187 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00188}00188 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ \(\backslash\)c GeneralisedElement::ndof\_types() must return the number of dof types}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00189}00189 \textcolor{comment}{  associated with an element.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00190}00190 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ \(\backslash\)c GeneralisedElement::get\_dof\_numbers\_for\_unknowns(...) must return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00191}00191 \textcolor{comment}{  a list of pairs comprising a map from global equation number to }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00192}00192 \textcolor{comment}{  dof type for all unknowns in the element.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00193}00193 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00194}00194 \textcolor{comment}{These are already implemented for many elements. If not, the functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00195}00195 \textcolor{comment}{are easy to write. For instance, \(\backslash\)c oomph-\/lib's <c>DIM</c>-\/dimensional }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00196}00196 \textcolor{comment}{linear elasticity elements from the \(\backslash\)c QLinearElasticityElement family}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00197}00197 \textcolor{comment}{can be made block-\/preconditionable by using the following}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00198}00198 \textcolor{comment}{wrapper class:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00199}00199 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00200}00200 \textcolor{comment}{\(\backslash\)dontinclude two\_d\_linear\_elasticity\_with\_simple\_block\_diagonal\_preconditioner.cc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00201}00201 \textcolor{comment}{\(\backslash\)skipline  start\_of\_mylinearelasticityelement}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00202}00202 \textcolor{comment}{\(\backslash\)until \};}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00203}00203 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00204}00204 \textcolor{comment}{Thus, in the two-\/dimensional \(\backslash\)c MyLinearElasticityElement<2> we }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00205}00205 \textcolor{comment}{have two types of dofs, corresponding to the displacements in the }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00206}00206 \textcolor{comment}{\(\backslash\)f\$x\(\backslash\)f\$ and \(\backslash\)f\$ y \(\backslash\)f\$ directions, respectively. They are enumerated }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00207}00207 \textcolor{comment}{as dof types 0 and 1, respectively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00208}00208 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00209}00209 \textcolor{comment}{\(\backslash\)subsection dof\_types\_and\_block\_types dof types, blocks, compound blocks and meshes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00210}00210 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00211}00211 \textcolor{comment}{In the block diagonal preconditioner for the two-\/dimensional linear}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00212}00212 \textcolor{comment}{elasticity problem, discussed above, we have dof types that }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00213}00213 \textcolor{comment}{correspond directly to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00214}00214 \textcolor{comment}{the blocks in the (re-\/ordered) Jacobian matrix. However, as we will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00215}00215 \textcolor{comment}{demonstrate <a href="{}\#compound"{}>below</a>, it is also }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00216}00216 \textcolor{comment}{possible to combine the blocks associated with multiple dofs into a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00217}00217 \textcolor{comment}{single (compound) block in which case the number of blocks is smaller than the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00218}00218 \textcolor{comment}{number of dof types. The relationship between dof types, block types, }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00219}00219 \textcolor{comment}{the elemental dof type classification and meshes are as follows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00220}00220 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00221}00221 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ \(\backslash\)b Elemental \(\backslash\)b dof \(\backslash\)b type \(\backslash\)b classification: Each element}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00222}00222 \textcolor{comment}{  classifies its own dof types in the function }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00223}00223 \textcolor{comment}{  \(\backslash\)c get\_dof\_numbers\_for\_unknowns(...). In the case of the two-\/dimensional}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00224}00224 \textcolor{comment}{  \(\backslash\)c MyLinearElasticityElement<2> elements, the dof types are classified}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00225}00225 \textcolor{comment}{  as \(\backslash\)c 0 and \(\backslash\)c 1; for two-\/dimensional \(\backslash\)c QTaylorHoodElement<2> }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00226}00226 \textcolor{comment}{  Navier-\/Stokes }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00227}00227 \textcolor{comment}{  elements, the dof types}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00228}00228 \textcolor{comment}{  are classified as \(\backslash\)c 0 and \(\backslash\)c 1 for the \(\backslash\)f\$ x \(\backslash\)f\$ and \(\backslash\)f\$y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00229}00229 \textcolor{comment}{  \(\backslash\)f\$-\/velocities, and \(\backslash\)c 2 for the pressure \(\backslash\)f\$ p \(\backslash\)f\$; etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00230}00230 \textcolor{comment}{  \(\backslash\)n\(\backslash\)n}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00231}00231 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ \(\backslash\)b Role \(\backslash\)b of \(\backslash\)b meshes: When classifying the degrees of freedom into}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00232}00232 \textcolor{comment}{  dof types, the block preconditioning framework}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00233}00233 \textcolor{comment}{  visits all elements that make contributions to the Jacobian matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00234}00234 \textcolor{comment}{  and associates the global equation number of each dof with the dof type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00235}00235 \textcolor{comment}{  specified by the element. The block preconditioning framework is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00236}00236 \textcolor{comment}{  given access to the elements via (possibly multiple) meshes (here}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00237}00237 \textcolor{comment}{  simply interpreted as containers for elements), each of }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00238}00238 \textcolor{comment}{  which is assumed to contain elements of a single type. The total}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00239}00239 \textcolor{comment}{  number of dof types in the block preconditioner is the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00240}00240 \textcolor{comment}{  sum of the dof types of the elements in the meshes. For}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00241}00241 \textcolor{comment}{  instance, in a 2D fluid-\/structure interaction problem we have two}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00242}00242 \textcolor{comment}{  different element types, the solid elements (which contain the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00243}00243 \textcolor{comment}{  \(\backslash\)f\$ x \(\backslash\)f\$ and \(\backslash\)f\$ y\(\backslash\)f\$ solid displacements, \(\backslash\)f\$ u\_x \(\backslash\)f\$ and \(\backslash\)f\$}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00244}00244 \textcolor{comment}{  u\_y \(\backslash\)f\$, respectively, assumed to be }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00245}00245 \textcolor{comment}{  enumerated as dof types}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00246}00246 \textcolor{comment}{  0 and 1 by these elements) and the fluid elements (which contain the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00247}00247 \textcolor{comment}{  \(\backslash\)f\$ x \(\backslash\)f\$-\/ and \(\backslash\)f\$ y \(\backslash\)f\$ -\/ fluid velocities, \(\backslash\)f\$ v\_x \(\backslash\)f\$ and \(\backslash\)f\$ v\_y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00248}00248 \textcolor{comment}{  \(\backslash\)f\$ ,  and the pressure, \(\backslash\)f\$ p \(\backslash\)f\$, assumed to }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00249}00249 \textcolor{comment}{  be enumerated as dof types}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00250}00250 \textcolor{comment}{  0, 1 and 2 by these elements). Assuming the mesh of solid elements}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00251}00251 \textcolor{comment}{  is specified as mesh 0 and the mesh of fluid elements is mesh 1, the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00252}00252 \textcolor{comment}{  block preconditioner has a total of five dof types which represent,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00253}00253 \textcolor{comment}{  in order, \(\backslash\)f\$ u\_x, u\_y, v\_x, v\_y, p\(\backslash\)f\$. Note that if certain degrees of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00254}00254 \textcolor{comment}{  freedom are classified by multiple elements, the most recent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00255}00255 \textcolor{comment}{  assignment of the dof type over-\/writes previous assignments.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00256}00256 \textcolor{comment}{  The order in which meshes are specified therefore matters. }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00257}00257 \textcolor{comment}{  \(\backslash\)n}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00258}00258 \textcolor{comment}{  A corollary to this is that a block preconditioner does not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00259}00259 \textcolor{comment}{  need to "{}know"{} about elements that do not introduce any new }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00260}00260 \textcolor{comment}{  unknowns. For instance, \(\backslash\)c FaceElements that apply Neumann/flux }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00261}00261 \textcolor{comment}{  boundary conditions operate on dofs that are already}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00262}00262 \textcolor{comment}{  contained in (and therefore classified by) the elements in the }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00263}00263 \textcolor{comment}{  "{}bulk"{} mesh. Conversely, if a \(\backslash\)c FaceElement}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00264}00264 \textcolor{comment}{  imposes a boundary condition via Lagrange-\/multipliers, the dofs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00265}00265 \textcolor{comment}{  that represent these Lagrange multipliers must be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00266}00266 \textcolor{comment}{  classified by the \(\backslash\)c FaceElements since the "{}bulk elements"{} are not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00267}00267 \textcolor{comment}{  aware of them. }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00268}00268 \textcolor{comment}{  \(\backslash\)n}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00269}00269 \textcolor{comment}{  If \(\backslash\)c oomph-\/lib is compiled with the \(\backslash\)c PARANOID flag, }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00270}00270 \textcolor{comment}{  an error is thrown if any of the global unknowns are not associated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00271}00271 \textcolor{comment}{  with a dof type.\(\backslash\)n\(\backslash\)n}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00272}00272 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ \(\backslash\)b Blocks: The blocks are the sub-\/blocks of the system matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00273}00273 \textcolor{comment}{  (usually the Jacobian matrix from the Newton method) that the block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00274}00274 \textcolor{comment}{  preconditioner works with. By default, each block is associated with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00275}00275 \textcolor{comment}{  exactly one dof type. However, it is possible create "{}compound blocks"{} that }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00276}00276 \textcolor{comment}{  are associated with more than one dof type. For example, in the }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00277}00277 \textcolor{comment}{  Navier-\/Stokes LSC preconditioner (in 2D) we have three dof }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00278}00278 \textcolor{comment}{  types (the \(\backslash\)f\$x\(\backslash\)f\$ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00279}00279 \textcolor{comment}{  \(\backslash\)f\$y\(\backslash\)f\$-\/velocities and the pressure), but the preconditioner works with }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00280}00280 \textcolor{comment}{  just two block types (forming the velocity and pressure blocks). The setup}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00281}00281 \textcolor{comment}{  of the block types is handled by the function \(\backslash\)c block\_setup(...) discussed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00282}00282 \textcolor{comment}{  below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00283}00283 \textcolor{comment}{.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00284}00284 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00285}00285 \textcolor{comment}{\(\backslash\)section multi\_poisson Simple preconditioner examples}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00286}00286 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00287}00287 \textcolor{comment}{We will now illustrate the capabilities of the block preconditioning}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00288}00288 \textcolor{comment}{framework by considering the system of \(\backslash\)f\$ N \(\backslash\)f\$ coupled PDEs }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00289}00289 \textcolor{comment}{\(\backslash\)f[ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00290}00290 \textcolor{comment}{\(\backslash\)left( \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)partial\string^2 u\_i\}\{\(\backslash\)partial x\_j\string^2\} }}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00638}00638 \textcolor{comment}{  The setup and application of this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00639}00639 \textcolor{comment}{  preconditioner is obviously much faster than for the \(\backslash\)c}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00640}00640 \textcolor{comment}{  SuperLUPreconditioner. Its setup merely requires the extraction of the }}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00843}00843 \textcolor{comment}{\(\backslash\)subsubsection two\_plus\_three\_theory Theory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00844}00844 \textcolor{comment}{So far we have illustrated how to implement block preconditioners }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00845}00845 \textcolor{comment}{for cases where the dof types (as identified by the elements) }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00846}00846 \textcolor{comment}{correspond directly to }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00847}00847 \textcolor{comment}{the block types. This is appropriate for our model PDE system }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00848}00848 \textcolor{comment}{(1) in which the five fields (and the governing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00849}00849 \textcolor{comment}{equations) are all of the same type. In many applications,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00850}00850 \textcolor{comment}{particularly in multi-\/physics problems, it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00851}00851 \textcolor{comment}{may be desirable to combine similar/related dof types into single}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00852}00852 \textcolor{comment}{blocks. For instance, in a 2D fluid-\/structure interaction problem,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00853}00853 \textcolor{comment}{we may wish to distinguish between the two solid (x and y solid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00854}00854 \textcolor{comment}{displacements) and three fluid (x and y fluid velocities and the pressure)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l02019}02019 \textcolor{comment}{is used as a subsidiary block preconditioner in an FSI problem that }}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l02021}02021 \textcolor{comment}{(e.g. the two solid displacement components). This was done}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l02022}02022 \textcolor{comment}{by informing the subsidiary preconditioner which of the dof types}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l02023}02023 \textcolor{comment}{in the full-\/sized system to regard as "{}its own"{} when calling}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l02025}02025 \textcolor{comment}{This implies that the subsidiary block preconditioner remains unaware of any }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l02026}02026 \textcolor{comment}{ compound blocks that may have been formed in its master }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l02027}02027 \textcolor{comment}{ preconditioner. The functionality presented so far only allows us}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l02028}02028 \textcolor{comment}{to associate dof-\/blocks in the master preconditioner with dof}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l02029}02029 \textcolor{comment}{blocks in the subsidiary block preconditioner.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l02030}02030 \textcolor{comment}{It is therefore not possible (without further functionality which we explain}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l02031}02031 \textcolor{comment}{in this example) to use a subsidiary block preconditioner if the dof-\/types}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l02032}02032 \textcolor{comment}{in the master preconditioner are "{}too fine-\/grained"{}. This arises,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l02033}02033 \textcolor{comment}{for instance, in Navier-\/Stokes problems where the master preconditioner}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l02034}02034 \textcolor{comment}{sub-\/divides the two components of the fluid velocity into degrees of freedom}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l02035}02035 \textcolor{comment}{on the domain boundary and those in the interior. It is then necessary}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l02036}02036 \textcolor{comment}{to make the subsidiary preconditioner act on the combined }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioners_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l02037}02037 \textcolor{comment}{dof types, a process that we describe as "{}coarsening"{}.}}
